          }), _jsx(FileTreeViewerFile, {
            name: "cli.py",
            path: "./src/video2notes/cli.py",
            fileType: "code",
            publicHrefPath: "posts/AI-Video2Text/src/video2notes/cli.py",
            codeText: "﻿\"\"\"video2notes CLI: batch transcribe and screenshot video courses.\"\"\"\n\nimport argparse\nimport os\nimport sys\nimport time\nfrom tqdm import tqdm\n\n\ndef _safe_folder_name(name: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Sanitize a string for use as a folder name.\"\"\"\n    return \"\".join(c if c.isalnum() or c in \" -_().[]\" else \"_\" for c in name).strip()\n\n\ndef _detect_cuda() -> str:\n    try:\n        import torch\n        return \"cuda\" if torch.cuda.is_available() else \"cpu\"\n    except Exception:\n        return \"cpu\"\n\n\ndef process_video(\n    video_path: str,\n    output_dir: str,\n    model_name: str = \"tiny\",\n    device: str = \"cpu\",\n    interval: int = 120,\n    language: str | None = None,\n    skip_existing: bool = True,\n) -> bool:\n    \"\"\"Process a single video: transcribe + screenshot + markdown.\n\n    Returns True if processing succeeded (or was skipped).\n    \"\"\"\n    from .transcriber import transcribe, save_srt\n    from .screenshotter import get_duration, extract_screenshots\n    from .markdown_gen import generate_markdown\n\n    vname = os.path.splitext(os.path.basename(video_path))[0]\n    safe = _safe_folder_name(vname)\n    out_dir = os.path.join(output_dir, safe)\n    srt_file = os.path.join(out_dir, \"subtitle.srt\")\n    ss_dir = os.path.join(out_dir, \"screenshots\")\n    md_file = os.path.join(out_dir, \"notes.md\")\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 60}\")\n    print(f\"  Video: {vname}\")\n    print(f\"  Out:   {out_dir}\")\n    os.makedirs(out_dir, exist_ok=True)\n\n    srt_ok = os.path.isfile(srt_file) and os.path.getsize(srt_file) > 0\n    ss_ok = os.path.isdir(ss_dir) and len(os.listdir(ss_dir)) > 0\n\n    if skip_existing and srt_ok and ss_ok:\n        print(\"  [SKIP] Already processed\")\n        return True\n\n    # Step 1: Transcribe\n    if not srt_ok:\n        result = transcribe(video_path, model_name=model_name, device=device, language=language, verbose=False)\n        save_srt(result, srt_file)\n    else:\n        print(\"  [1/2] SRT exists, skipping\")\n\n    # Step 2: Screenshots\n    if not ss_ok:\n        print(f\"  [2/2] Extracting screenshots every {interval}s...\")\n        duration = get_duration(video_path)\n        if duration:\n            print(f\"    Duration: {duration / 60:.1f} min\")\n            cnt = extract_screenshots(video_path, ss_dir, duration, interval=interval)\n            print(f\"    Captured {cnt} screenshots\")\n        else:\n            print(\"    [WARN] Cannot determine duration, skipping screenshots\")\n    else:\n        print(\"  [2/2] Screenshots exist, skipping\")\n\n    # Step 3: Generate markdown (always regenerate if both exist)\n    if os.path.isfile(srt_file) and os.path.isdir(ss_dir):\n        content = generate_markdown(out_dir)\n        with open(md_file, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            f.write(content)\n        print(f\"  [3/3] notes.md generated ({len(content)} chars)\")\n\n    return True\n\n\ndef main():\n    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(\n        description=\"video2notes - extract subtitles and screenshots from video courses\",\n        formatter_class=argparse.RawDescriptionHelpFormatter,\n        epilog=(\n            \"Examples:\\n\"\n            \"  # Process a single video directory\\n\"\n            \"  video2notes -i D:\\\\Videos\\\\course -o D:\\\\Output\\\\course\\n\\n\"\n            \"  # Use GPU and medium model\\n\"\n            \"  video2notes -i D:\\\\Videos\\\\course -o D:\\\\Output\\\\course --device cuda --model medium\\n\\n\"\n            \"  # Only regenerate markdown from existing SRT + screenshots\\n\"\n            \"  video2notes -o D:\\\\Output\\\\course --markdown-only\\n\"\n        ),\n    )\n\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"-i\", \"--input-dir\",\n        default=None,\n        help=\"Directory containing video files\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"-o\", \"--output-dir\",\n        required=True,\n        help=\"Root output directory (one subfolder per video)\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--model\",\n        default=\"tiny\",\n        help=\"Whisper model name (tiny/base/small/medium/large) or path to a .pt model file (default: tiny)\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--device\",\n        default=None,\n        choices=[\"cpu\", \"cuda\"],\n        help=f\"Compute device (default: auto-detect, currently: {_detect_cuda()})\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--language\",\n        default=None,\n        help=\"Language code (e.g. 'zh' for Chinese). Auto-detected for Chinese keywords\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--interval\",\n        type=int,\n        default=120,\n        help=\"Screenshot interval in seconds (default: 120 = 2 minutes)\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--force\",\n        action=\"store_true\",\n        help=\"Re-process all videos even if already done\",\n    )\n    parser.add_argument(\n        \"--markdown-only\",\n        action=\"store_true\",\n        help=\"Only regenerate notes.md from existing SRT + screenshots (no -i needed)\",\n    )\n\n    args = parser.parse_args()\n\n    if args.markdown_only:\n        from .markdown_gen import generate_all\n        output_base = os.path.normpath(args.output_dir)\n        if not os.path.isdir(output_base):\n            print(f\"ERROR: Output directory not found: {output_base}\")\n            sys.exit(1)\n        print(f\"Markdown-only mode: regenerating notes.md under {output_base}\")\n        generate_all(output_base)\n        return\n\n    # Normal mode: transcribe + screenshot\n    if not args.input_dir:\n        print(\"ERROR: --input-dir is required (or use --markdown-only)\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n    if not os.path.isdir(args.input_dir):\n        print(f\"ERROR: Input directory not found: {args.input_dir}\")\n        sys.exit(1)\n\n    import torch\n    device = args.device or _detect_cuda()\n\n    # Build output directory name from input dir\n    dir_name = os.path.basename(os.path.normpath(args.input_dir))\n    safe = _safe_folder_name(dir_name)\n    output_base = os.path.join(args.output_dir, safe)\n    os.makedirs(output_base, exist_ok=True)\n\n    videos = sorted(\n        f for f in os.listdir(args.input_dir)\n        if f.lower().endswith((\".mp4\", \".mkv\", \".avi\", \".mov\"))\n    )\n\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 60}\")\n    print(f\"  Input:     {args.input_dir}\")\n    print(f\"  Output:    {output_base}\")\n    print(f\"  Videos:    {len(videos)} found\")\n    print(f\"  Model:     {args.model}\")\n    print(f\"  Device:    {device}\")\n    print(f\"  Interval:  {args.interval}s\")\n    print(f\"  Language:  {args.language or 'auto'}\")\n    print(f\"{'=' * 60}\\n\")\n\n    print(f\"CUDA available: {torch.cuda.is_available()}\")\n    if torch.cuda.is_available():\n        print(f\"GPU: {torch.cuda.get_device_name(0)}\")\n\n    start_time = time.time()\n    done = 0\n    skip_existing = not args.force\n\n    pbar = tqdm(videos, desc=\"Processing videos\", unit=\"video\")\n    for idx, v in enumerate(pbar, 1):\n        vp = os.path.join(args.input_dir, v)\n        pbar.set_postfix_str(v)\n        try:\n            ok = process_video(\n                video_path=vp,\n                output_dir=output_base,\n                model_name=args.model,\n                device=device,\n                interval=args.interval,\n                language=args.language,\n                skip_existing=skip_existing,\n            )\n            if ok:\n                done += 1\n        except Exception as ex:\n            tqdm.write(f\"  [ERROR] {ex}\")\n            import traceback\n            traceback.print_exc()\n\n        with open(os.path.join(output_base, \"_progress.txt\"), \"w\") as pf:\n            pf.write(f\"Completed: {idx}/{len(videos)}\\nLast: {v}\\n\")\n\n    elapsed = time.time() - start_time\n    print(f\"\\n{'=' * 60}\")\n    print(f\"  Done: {done}/{len(videos)} videos in {elapsed / 3600:.1f}h\")\n    print(f\"  Output: {output_base}\")\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n",

int(sec)) * 1000)\n    return f\"{h:02d}:{m:02d}:{s:02d},{ms:03d}\"\n\n\ndef transcribe(\n    video_path: str,\n    model_name: str = \"tiny\",\n    device: str = \"cuda\" if torch.cuda.is_available() else \"cpu\",\n    language: str | None = None,\n    verbose: bool = False,\n) -> dict:\n    \"\"\"Transcribe a video file with Whisper, return result dict.\"\"\"\n    if language is None:\n        language = _detect_language(video_path)\n\n    print(f\"  Loading whisper model '{model_name}'...\")\n    t0 = time.time()\n    model = whisper.load_model(model_name)\n    if device == \"cuda\" and torch.cuda.is_available():\n        model = model.cuda()\n    print(f\"    Loaded in {time.time() - t0:.1f}s\")\n\n    print(f\"  Transcribing (device={device}, lang={language or 'auto'})...\")\n    ts = time.time()\n    result = model.transcribe(\n        video_path,\n        language=language,\n        verbose=verbose,\n        fp16=(device == \"cuda\"),\n    )\n    elapsed = time.time() - ts\n    print(f\"    Done in {elapsed / 60:.1f} min, {len(result['segments'])} segments\")\n    return result\n\n\ndef save_srt(result: dict, srt_path: str):\n    \"\"\"Save transcription result as SRT file.\"\"\"\n    os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(srt_path), exist_ok=True)\n    with open(srt_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        for i, seg in enumerate(result[\"segments\"], 1):\n            f.write(f\"{i}\\n\")\n            f.write(f\"{_format_srt_timestamp(seg['start'])} --> {_format_srt_timestamp(seg['end'])}\\n\")\n            f.write(f\"{seg['text'].strip()}\\n\\n\")\n    print(f\"    SRT saved: {srt_path}\")\n",

tqdm\n\nFFMPEG_PATH = imageio_ffmpeg.get_ffmpeg_exe()\n\n\ndef get_duration(video_path: str) -> float | None:\n    \"\"\"Get video duration in seconds using OpenCV.\"\"\"\n    cap = cv2.VideoCapture(video_path)\n    if not cap.isOpened():\n        return None\n    fps = cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FPS)\n    fc = int(cap.get(cv2.CAP_PROP_FRAME_COUNT))\n    cap.release()\n    return fc / fps if fps > 0 else None\n\n\ndef extract_screenshots(\n    video_path: str,\n    output_dir: str,\n    duration: float,\n    interval: int = 120,\n    quality: int = 2,\n) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Extract screenshots every `interval` seconds.\n\n    Args:\n        video_path: Path to the video file.\n        output_dir: Directory to save screenshots.\n        duration: Video duration in seconds.\n        interval: Screenshot interval in seconds (default 120 = 2 min).\n        quality: ffmpeg -q:v quality (2 = ~90% JPEG quality).\n\n    Returns:\n        Number of screenshots captured.\n    \"\"\"\n    os.makedirs(output_dir, exist_ok=True)\n    count = 0\n    times = list(range(interval, int(duration), interval))\n\n    for t in tqdm(times, desc=\"  Screenshots\", unit=\"img\", leave=False):\n        fname = f\"{t // 60:02d}_{t % 60:02d}.jpg\"\n        fpath = os.path.join(output_dir, fname)\n        if os.path.exists(fpath):\n            count += 1\n            continue\n\n        subprocess.run(\n            [\n                FFMPEG_PATH, \"-y\",\n                \"-ss\", str(t),\n                \"-i\", video_path,\n                \"-vframes\", \"1\",\n                \"-q:v\", str(quality),\n                \"-f\", \"image2\",\n                fpath,\n            ],\n            capture_output=True,\n            timeout=60,\n        )\n        if os.path.exists(fpath):\n            count += 1\n\n    return count\n",

\"\"\"Convert SRT timestamp (HH:MM:SS,mmm) to total seconds.\"\"\"\n    h, m, s = ts.replace(\",\", \".\").split(\":\")\n    return int(h) * 3600 + int(m) * 60 + float(s)\n\n\ndef parse_srt(srt_path: str) -> list[tuple[float, float, str]]:\n    \"\"\"Parse SRT file into list of (start_sec, end_sec, text) tuples.\"\"\"\n    segments = []\n    with open(srt_path, \"r\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        content = f.read()\n    blocks = content.strip().split(\"\\n\\n\")\n    for block in blocks:\n        lines = block.strip().split(\"\\n\")\n        if len(lines) < 3:\n            continue\n        time_line = lines[1]\n        if \"-->\" not in time_line:\n            continue\n        parts = time_line.split(\" --> \")\n        if len(parts) != 2:\n            continue\n        start = _srt_time_to_seconds(parts[0].strip())\n        end = _srt_time_to_seconds(parts[1].strip())\n        text = \" \".join(l.strip() for l in lines[2:])\n        segments.append((start, end, text))\n    return segments\n\n\ndef _format_time(seconds: int) -> str:\n    return f\"{seconds // 60:02d}:{seconds % 60:02d}\"\n\n\ndef _parse_screenshot_name(name: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"Parse 'MM_SS.jpg' to total seconds.\"\"\"\n    base = os.path.splitext(name)[0]\n    parts = base.split(\"_\")\n    return int(parts[0]) * 60 + int(parts[1]) if len(parts) == 2 else 0\n\n\ndef generate_markdown(video_folder: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Generate a notes.md string for one video folder.\n\n    The markdown interleaves subtitle text with screenshots every 2-minute interval.\n    \"\"\"\n    srt_path = os.path.join(video_folder, \"subtitle.srt\")\n    ss_dir = os.path.join(video_folder, \"screenshots\")\n    video_name = os.path.basename(video_folder)\n\n    segments = parse_srt(srt_path)\n    screenshots = sorted(\n        [f for f in os.listdir(ss_dir) if f.endswith(\".jpg\")],\n        key=lambda f: _parse_screenshot_name(f),\n    )\n\n    if not segments:\n        return f\"# {video_name}\\n\\n*(No subtitle content)*\\n\"\n    if not screenshots:\n        lines = [f\"# {video_name}\\n\"]\n        for start, end, text in segments:\n            lines.append(f\"- **{_format_time(int(start))} - {_format_time(int(end))}**: {text}\")\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\n    lines = [f\"# {video_name}\\n\"]\n    ss_index = 0\n    screenshot_times = [_parse_screenshot_name(f) for f in screenshots]\n\n    for start, end, text in segments:\n        inserted = False\n        while ss_index < len(screenshot_times):\n            ss_time = screenshot_times[ss_index]\n            interval_end = ss_time\n            interval_start = ss_time - 120 if ss_time >= 120 else 0\n\n            if start < interval_end and end > interval_start:\n                lines.append(f\"\\n## {_format_time(interval_start)} - {_format_time(interval_end)}\\n\")\n                lines.append(f\"{text}\\n\")\n                ss_rel = os.path.join(\"screenshots\", screenshots[ss_index])\n                lines.append(f\"![Screenshot at {_format_time(ss_time)}]({ss_rel})\\n\")\n                ss_index += 1\n                inserted = True\n                break\n            elif ss_time <= start:\n                interval_start = max(0, ss_time - 120)\n                interval_end = ss_time\n                lines.append(f\"\\n## {_format_time(interval_start)} - {_format_time(interval_end)}\\n\")\n                lines.append(\"*(No speech in this interval)*\\n\")\n                ss_rel = os.path.join(\"screenshots\", screenshots[ss_index])\n                lines.append(f\"![Screenshot at {_format_time(ss_time)}]({ss_rel})\\n\")\n                ss_index += 1\n            else:\n                break\n        if not inserted:\n            lines.append(f\"{text}\\n\")\n\n    while ss_index < len(screenshot_times):\n        ss_time = screenshot_times[ss_index]\n        interval_start = max(0, ss_time - 120)\n        interval_end = ss_time\n        lines.append(f\"\\n## {_format_time(interval_start)} - {_format_time(interval_end)}\\n\")\n        lines.append(\"*(No speech in this interval)*\\n\")\n        ss_rel = os.path.join(\"screenshots\", screenshots[ss_index])\n        lines.append(f\"![Screenshot at {_format_time(ss_time)}]({ss_rel})\\n\")\n        ss_index += 1\n\n    return \"\".join(lines)\n\n\ndef generate_all(output_base: str):\n    \"\"\"Walk output_base and regenerate notes.md for every video folder.\"\"\"\n    folders = []\n    for root, dirs, files in os.walk(output_base):\n        if \"subtitle.srt\" in files and \"screenshots\" in dirs:\n            folders.append(root)\n\n    for folder in tqdm(sorted(folders), desc=\"Generating markdown\", unit=\"folder\"):\n        md_path = os.path.join(folder, \"notes.md\")\n        content = generate_markdown(folder)\n        with open(md_path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            f.write(content)\n    tqdm.write(f\"Done! Generated {len(folders)} markdown files\")\n",

function MDXContent(props = {}) {
  const {wrapper: MDXLayout} = {
    ..._provideComponents(),
    ...props.components
  };
  return MDXLayout ? _jsx(MDXLayout, {
    ...props,
    children: _jsx(_createMdxContent, {
      ...props
    })
  }) : _createMdxContent(props);
}
return {
  default: MDXContent
};
